class=\"frame-title\">Cheatsheet</h2><div ng-if=\"!(calc.doc.metaInputs.length &amp;&amp; calc.doc.metaOutputs.length)\" class=\"content\"><p>Not so fast! First add some <span ng-if=\"!calc.doc.metaInputs.length &amp;&amp; calc.doc.metaOutputs.length\">inputs</span><span ng-if=\"calc.doc.metaInputs.length &amp;&amp; !calc.doc.metaOutputs.length\">outputs</span><span ng-if=\"!calc.doc.metaInputs.length &amp;&amp; !calc.doc.metaOutputs.length\">inputs and outputs</span> in the IO tab.</p></div><div ng-if=\"calc.doc.metaInputs.length &amp;&amp; calc.doc.metaOutputs.length\" class=\"content\"><p>You need to write the body of a function that transforms inputs into outputs:</p><pre>function(inputs) {\n  [Your script goes here]\n} -> outputs</pre><p>where <code>inputs</code> is an object like this:</p><pre>{{getInputsSchema()}}</pre><p>and the returned value is an object like this:</p><pre>{{getOutputsSchema()}}</pre><p>You can configure property names in both above objects in settings for specific inputs or outputs - this cheatsheet will update itself accordingly. You can omit some of the properties from the outputs object, in which case corresponding outputs will not be displayed. If you need an example, you can take a look at the <a href=\"https://jscalc.io/calc/X75idoIIszwv7VCZ\">calculator from the demo</a> (click the three dots next to \"Powered by JSCalc.io\", then \"Make a copy\").</p><p>The script will be run in a Web Worker. You can choose which libraries to use in calculator settings. If the script throws an error, its string representation will be displayed to the user, so you could write something like <code>throw 'Text to display'</code> .</p><p>Script editor keyboard shortcuts are listed <a href=\"https://github.com/ajaxorg/ace/wiki/Default-Keyboard-Shortcuts\" target=\"_blank\">on this page</a>, and you can also hit Cmd/Ctrl + S to save all changes in the calculator.</p></div></md-content></div></div><div ng-show=\"selectedTabIndex == 2\" flex=\"flex\" layout=\"column\" layout-fill=\"layout-fill\"><div id=\"share-container\" flex=\"flex\" layout-gt-md=\"row\" layout-fill=\"layout-fill\"><md-content id=\"link\" flex=\"flex\"><h2 class=\"frame-title\">Link</h2><div ng-show=\"newAndNotSaved\" class=\"link-title fade-in\">After you save this calculator, it will become available on the web at the following URL:</div><div ng-show=\"!newAndNotSaved\" class=\"link-title fade-in\">This calculator is published on the web at the following URL:</div><div class=\"link\"><a href=\"/calc/{{calcId}}\">https://jscalc.io/calc/{{calcId}}</a></div><div class=\"description-title\">Description</div><div class=\"md-caption\">Text to display below the title, 1-2 sentences recommended. You can include URLs and emails – they will be automatically converted into links. Line breaks will be ignored. This text will also be used in the 'description' meta tag, so search engines would normally display it in search results.</div><div layout=\"column\" class=\"textarea-container\"><textarea columns=\"1\" ng-model=\"calc.doc.description\" aria-label=\"Description\"></textarea></div></md-content><md-content id=\"embed\" flex=\"flex\"><h2 class=\"frame-title\">Embed</h2><div><md-checkbox ng-model=\"focusFirstInput\" class=\"md-primary\">Set focus on the first input when the page is opened.</md-checkbox></div><div ng-show=\"newAndNotSaved\" class=\"fade-in\">Save the calculator, then paste this code to embed on your website or blog:</div><div ng-show=\"!newAndNotSaved\" class=\"fade-in\">Paste this code to embed on your website or blog:</div><div layout=\"column\" class=\"textarea-container\"><textarea columns=\"1\" aria-label=\"Embed code to copy\" readonly=\"readonly\" class=\"code\"><iframe src=\"https://jscalc.io/embed/{{calcId}}{{focusFirstInput ?
